[30;1m28 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m29 | [0m[35mThe Simple JWT blacklist app implements its outstanding and blacklisted token[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35mlists using two models: ``OutstandingToken`` and ``BlacklistedToken``.  Model[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35madmins are defined for both of these models.  To add a token to the blacklist,[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35mfind its corresponding ``OutstandingToken`` record in the admin and use the[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35madmin again to create a ``BlacklistedToken`` record that points to the[0m
